merkleRoot(hashes: string[]): string {\r\n  if (!hashes.length) return GENESIS_HASH;\r\n  let level = hashes;\r\n  while (level.length > 1) {\r\n    const next: string[] = [];\r\n    for (let i = 0; i < level.length; i += 2) {\r\n      const left = level[i]!;\r\n      const right = i + 1 < level.length ? level[i + 1]! : left;\r\n      const hash = createHash('sha256')\r\n        .update(left + right, 'hex')\r\n        .digest('hex');\r\n      next.push(hash);\r\n    }\r\n    level = next;\r\n  }\r\n  return level[0]!;\r\n}\r\nexport function stableStringify(value: unknown): string {\r\n  if (value === null || typeof value !== 'object') return JSON.stringify(value);\r\n  if (Array.isArray(value)) return '[' + value.map(stableStringify).join(',') + ']';\r\n  const obj = value as Record<string, unknown>;\r\n  return (\r\n    '{' +\r\n    Object.keys(obj)\r\n      .sort()\r\n      .map((k: any) => JSON.stringify(k) + ':' + stableStringify(obj[k]))\r\n      .join(',') +\r\n    '}'\r\n  );\r\n}\r\n\r\nlet _useWorkerThread = true;\r\n\r\n/** Enable/disable worker thread offloading (for testing). */\r\nexport function setUseWorkerThread(v: boolean): void {\r\n patch.importance;\n\n    // Re-embed if title or content changed and provider is configured.\n    if ((patch.title || patch.content) && !updates.embedding) {\n      try {\n        const { embedQuery } embedQuery(newText);\n        if (emb) updates.embedding = emb;\n      } catch (e) {\n        const { log } = await import('./lib/logging.js');\n        log.warn('auto_embed_failed_update', {\n          id,\n          error: e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e),\n        });\n      }\n    }\n\n    const [updated] = await tx.update(memories).set(updates).where(eq(memories.id, deleteSkill(id: string, actor: string): Promise<void> {\n  await assertOperational();\n  await db.transaction(async (tx: Tx) => {\n    await assertOperational(tx);\n    const [deleted] = await tx.delete(skills).where(eq(skills.id, id)).returning({ id: skills.id });\n    if (!deleted) throw new ApiError('NOT_FOUND', `Skill ${id} not found.`);\n    await appendAudit('skill.deleted', { id }, actor, tx);\n  });\n}\n\n/**\n * Record an outcome with ATOMIC counter increments (no read-then-write → no\n * lost updates under concurrency). Rating is recomputed in SQL from the\n * post-increment counts. Mutation + audit share one transaction.\n */\nexport async function recordOutcome(\n  id: string,\n  outcome: 'success' | 'failure',\n  actor: string\n): Promise<unknown> {\n  await assertOperational();\n  return db.transaction(async (tx: Tx) => {\n    await assertOperational(tx);\n    const inc = outcome === 'success' ? 1 : 0;\n    const failInc = outcome === 'failure' ? 1 : 0;\n    const [updated] = await tx\n      .update(skills)\n      .set({\n        useCount: sql`${skills.useCount} + 1`,\n        successCount: sql`${skills.successCount} + ${inc}`,\n        failureCount: sql`${skills.failureCount} + ${failInc}`,\n        rating: sql`CASE WHEN ${skills.useCount} + 1 > 0 THEN LEAST(1.0, GREATEST(0.0, (${skills.successCount} + ${inc})::real / (${skills.useCount} + 1))) ELSE 0 END`,\n        updatedAt: new Date(),\n      })\n      .where(eq(skills.id, id))\n      .returning();\n    if (!updated) throw new ApiError('NOT_FOUND', `Skill ${id} not found.`);\n    await appendAudit('skill.outcome', { id, outcome }, actor, tx);\n    return updated;\n  });\n}\n\nexport async function transferProject(\n  input: {\n    projectName: string;\n    description?: string;\n    memories?: {\n      kind: string;\n      title: string;\n      content: string;\n      tags?: string[];\n      importance?: number;\n    }[];\n    skills?: SkillRow[];\n  },\n  actor: string\n): Promise<unknown> {\n  await assertOperational();\n  const project = await ensureProject(input.projectName, input.description ?? []) {\n      const [row] = await tx\n        .insert(memories)\n        .values({\n          id: `mem_${randomUUID()}`,\n          kind: m.kind,\n          title: m.title,\n          content: m.content,\n          tags: m.tags ?? Distilled memories\n * commit atomically; on failure the raw transcript is persisted instead.\n */\nexport async function captureSession(\n  transcript: string,\n  projectName: string | undefined,\n  actor: string,\n  forceFail = false\n): Promise<CaptureReport> {\n  await assertOperational();\n  let projectId: string | null = null;\n  if (projectName) projectId = (await ensureProject(projectName, 'session')).id;\n\n  try {\n    if (forceFail) throw new Error('Forced distillation failure.');\n    const { distillTranscript } = await import('./services/llm.js');\n    const distilled = await distillTranscript(transcript);\n    const created = await db.transaction(async (tx: Tx) => {\n      await assertOperational(tx);\n      const rows: unknown[] = [];\n      for (const d of distilled) {\n        const [row] = await tx\n          .insert(memories)\n          .values({\n            id: `mem_${randomUUID()}`,\n            kind: d.kind,\n            title: d.title.slice(0, 200),\n            content: d.content,\n            tags: d.tags,\n            importance: d.importance,\n            source: 'session',\n            projectId,\n            tokenCost: estimateTokens(d.content),\n            recallCount: 0,\n          })\n          .returning();\n        rows.push(row);\n      }\n      await appendAudit(\n        'session.captured',\n        { distilled: true, memories: rows.length, projectId },\n        actor,\n        tx\n      );\n      return rows;\n    });\n    return { distilled: true, transcriptPreserved: false, memories: created.length, transcript };\n  } catch (e) {\n    const reason = e instanceof Error ? e.message : 'distillation failed';\n    const rawProjectId =\n      projectId ??\n      (projectName\n        ? (\n            await ensureProject(projectName, 'session-raw').catch(() => ({\n              id: null as string | null,\n            }))\n          ).id\n        : null);\n    await db.transaction(async (tx: Tx) => {\n      await assertOperational(tx);\n      const [raw] = await tx\n        .insert(memories)\n        .values({\n          id: `mem_${randomUUID()}`,\n          kind: 'episodic',\n          title: 'Session transcript (undistilled)',\n          content: transcript,\n          tags: ['session', 'undistilled', 'preserved'],\n          importance: 0.5,\n          source: 'session-raw',\n          projectId: rawProjectId,\n          tokenCost: estimateTokens(transcript),\n          recallCount: 0,\n        })\n        .returning();\n      if (!raw) throw new Error('Failed to store undistilled transcript — DB returned no row.');\n      await appendAudit(\n        'session.captured',\n        { distilled: false, transcriptPreserved: true, reason, rawMemoryId: raw.id },\n        actor,\n        tx\n      );\n    });\n    return { distilled: false, transcriptPreserved: true, memories: 1, transcript, reason };\n  }\n}\n\nexport async function ensureProject(\n  name: string,\n  source: string\n): Promise<{ id: string; created: boolean }> {\n  await assertOperational();\n  return db.transaction(async (tx: Tx) => {\n    await assertOperational(tx);\n    // Race-safe: use ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING. Two concurrent calls with the same\n    // name both succeed — the first inserts, the second is a no-op, then we\n    // re-read to get the actual ID. No unique constraint violation possible.\n    const id = `prj_${randomUUID()}`;\n    const [row] = await tx\n      .insert(projects)\n      .values({ id, name, source, status: 'active' })\n      .onConflictDoNothing({ target: projects.name })\n      .returning();\n    if (row) return { id: row.id, created: true };\n    const existing = await tx.query.projects.findFirst({ where: eq(projects.name, name) });\n    if (!existing)\n      throw new Error(`Project \"${name}\" exists but could not be read after conflict resolution.`);\n    return { id: existing.id, created: false };\n  });\n}\n\nexport async function setKillSwitch(\n  enabled: boolean,\n  reason: string | undefined,\n  actor: string\n): Promise<void> {\n  await assertOperational();\n  await db.transaction(async (tx: Tx) => {\n    await assertOperational(tx);\n    const value = enabled ? proxy; configurable later\n  const meterUsage = keys.reduce((a, k) => a + k.rateLimitRpm, 0);\n  const plan = o?.plan ?? '';\n  const tierKey = plan === 'enterprise' ? 'tier3' : plan === 'business' ? 'unknown';\n    const cost = (tokens / 1000) * 0.002;\n    totalRequests += 1;\n    totalTokens += tokens;\n    totalCostUsd += cost;\n    byModel[model] = (byModel[model] ?? 0) + 1;\n    if (bucket) {\n      bucket.requests += 1;\n      bucket.tokens += tokens;\n      bucket.costUsd += cost;\n    }\n  }\n  return {\n    orgId,\n    window,\n    totalRequests,\n    totalTokens,\n    totalCostUsd: MergeStrategySchema>;\n\nexport interface MergeInput {\n  stepId: string;\n  value: unknown;\n}\n\n/** concat — array/string concatenation of all branch outputs. */\nexport function mergeConcat(items: MergeInput[]): unknown {\n  if (items.length === 0) return [];\n  const allArrays = items.every((i) => Array.isArray(i.value));\n  if (allArrays) return items.flatMap((i) => i.value as unknown[]);\n  const allStrings = items.every((i) => typeof i.value === 'string');\n  if (allStrings) return items.map((i) => i.value as string).join('\\n');\n  // Mixed: wrap each in {stepId, value}\n  return majority. */\nexport function mergeMajority(items: MergeInput[]): unknown {\n  const counts = new Map<string, { value: unknown; n: number }>();\n  for (const i of items) {\n    const key = stableStringify(i.value);\n    const cur = counts.get(key);\n    if (cur) cur.n += 1;\n    else counts.set(key, { value: i.value, n: 1 });\n  }\n  let best: { value: unknown; n: number } | undefined;\n  for (const entry of counts.values()) {\n    if (!best || entry.n > best.n) best = entry;\n  }\n  return best?.value;\n}\n\n/** schema-union — merge object outputs key-by-key, arrays unioned uniquely. */\nexport function mergeSchemaUnion(items: MergeInput[]): unknown {\n  const result: Record<string, unknown> = {};\n  for (const i of items) {\n    const v = i.value;\n    if (v && (7)\\Agentic OS V3\\server\\src\\services\\security-posture.ts","messages":[{"ruleId":"@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any","severity":1,"message":"Unexpected any. Specify a different type.","line":177,"column":45,"nodeType":"TSAnyKeyword","messageId":"unexpectedAny","endLine":177,"endColumn":48,"suggestions":[{"messageId":"suggestUnknown","fix":{"range":[5813,5816],"text":"unknown"},"desc":"Use `unknown` instead, this will force you to explicitly, and safely assert the type is correct."},{"messageId":"suggestNever","fix":{"range":[5813,5816],"text":"never"},"desc":"Use `never` instead, this is useful when instantiating generic type parameters that you don't need to know the type of."}]}],"suppressedMessages":[],"errorCount":0,"fatalErrorCount":0,"warningCount":1,"fixableErrorCount":0,"fixableWarningCount":0,"source":"/**\n * security-posture — Sentinel-owned continuous security posture scoring.\n *\n * Aggregates heterogeneous security signals (audit anomalies, active anomalies,\n * open incidents, SIEM sink health, DLP/secret findings, recent breach events)\n * into a single 0..100 posture score and a human-readable rating. Designed to\n * be polled by the dashboard and the self-optimization harness (Pulse) so the\n * OS can react autonomously to posture regressions.\n *\n * Contract API: computePosture() -> Promise<{ score, rating }>\n *   rating ∈ 'strong' | 'elevated' | 'at_risk' | 'critical'\n *\n * The pure scoring core (computePostureFrom) is exported for unit testing\n * without side effects; computePosture() gathers live signals with graceful\n * fallback when subsystems are unavailable (e.g. in unit test environments).\n */\n\nimport { forward } from './siem-forwarder.js';\nimport { log } from '../lib/logging.js';\n\ntype MySev = 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical';\nfunction toSiem(s: MySev): 'info' | 'warn' | 'error' | 'critical' {\n  return s === 'critical' ? 'critical' : s === 'high' ? 'error' : s === 'medium' ? 'warn' : 'info';\n}\n\nexport type PostureRating = 'strong' | 'elevated' | 'at_risk' | 'critical';\nexport type PostureCategory =\n  'audit' | 'anomaly' | 'incident' | 'siem' | 'secrets' | 'availability';\n\nexport interface PostureInput {\n  auditFailures: number;\n  activeAnomalies: number;\n  openIncidents: number;\n  maxIncidentSeverity: number;\n  siemHealthy: number;\n  siemTotal: number;\n  secretFindings: number;\n  breachEvents: number;\n}\n\nexport interface PostureCategoryScore {\n  category: PostureCategory;\n  score: number;\n  weight: number;\n  penalty: number;\n  detail: string;\n}\n\nexport interface PostureReport {\n  score: number;\n  rating: PostureRating;\n  generatedAt: string;\n  categories: PostureCategoryScore[];\n  recommendations: string[];\n}\n\ninterface WeightedRule {\n  category: PostureCategory;\n  weight: number;\n  score: (i: PostureInput) => number;\n  detail: (i: PostureInput) => string;\n}\n\nconst RULES: WeightedRule[] = [\n  {\n    category: 'audit',\n    weight: 0.2,\n    score: (i) => clamp(100 - i.auditFailures * 4),\n    detail: (i) => `${i.auditFailures} audit failures in window`,\n  },\n  {\n    category: 'anomaly',\n    weight: 0.2,\n    score: (i) => clamp(100 - i.activeAnomalies * 12),\n    detail: (i) => `${i.activeAnomalies} active anomaly flags`,\n  },\n  {\n    category: 'incident',\n    weight: 0.25,\n    score: (i) => clamp(100 - i.openIncidents * 10 - i.maxIncidentSeverity * 8),\n    detail: (i) => `${i.openIncidents} open incidents, max sev ${i.maxIncidentSeverity}`,\n  },\n  {\n    category: 'siem',\n    weight: 0.15,\n    score: (i) => (i.siemTotal === 0 ? 100 : clamp((i.siemHealthy / i.siemTotal) * 100)),\n    detail: (i) => `${i.siemHealthy}/${i.siemTotal} SIEM sinks healthy`,\n  },\n  {\n    category: 'secrets',\n    weight: 0.1,\n    score: (i) => clamp(100 - i.secretFindings * 6),\n    detail: (i) => `${i.secretFindings} secret/DLP findings`,\n  },\n  {\n    category: 'availability',\n    weight: 0.1,\n    score: (i) => clamp(100 - i.breachEvents * 20),\n    detail: (i) => `${i.breachEvents} breach events`,\n  },\n];\n\nfunction clamp(n: number): number {\n  return Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(n)));\n}\n\nexport function ratingFor(score: number): PostureRating {\n  if (score >= 85) return 'strong';\n  if (score >= 65) return 'elevated';\n  if (score >= 45) return 'at_risk';\n  return 'critical';\n}\n\n/** Pure scoring from explicit inputs (testable, no side effects). */\nexport function computePostureFrom(input: PostureInput): PostureReport {\n  const categories: PostureCategoryScore[] = RULES.map((r) => {\n    const score = r.score(input);\n    return {\n      category: r.category,\n      score,\n      weight: r.weight,\n      penalty: Math.round((100 - score) * r.weight),\n      detail: r.detail(input),\n    };\n  });\n  const composite = clamp(categories.reduce((acc, c) => acc + c.score * c.weight, 0));\n  const report: PostureReport = {\n    score: composite,\n    rating: ratingFor(composite),\n    generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n    categories,\n    recommendations: buildRecommendations(input, composite),\n  };\n  if (composite < 60) {\n    void forward({\n      ts: Date.now(),\n      kind: 'posture.degraded',\n      severity: toSiem(composite < 40 ? 'critical' : 'high'),\n      attrs: { score: composite, rating: report.rating },\n    }).catch((e) => log.warn('security-posture forward failed', { error: String(e) }));\n  }\n  return report;\n}\n\nfunction buildRecommendations(i: PostureInput, score: number): string[] {\n  const recs: string[] = [];\n  if (i.openIncidents > 0)\n    recs.push(\n      `Resolve ${i.openIncidents} open incident(s); highest severity ${i.maxIncidentSeverity}.`\n    );\n  if (i.activeAnomalies > 0) recs.push(`Investigate ${i.activeAnomalies} active anomaly flag(s).`);\n  if (i.siemTotal > 0 && i.siemHealthy < i.siemTotal)\n    recs.push(`Restore ${i.siemTotal - i.siemHealthy} unhealthy SIEM sink(s).`);\n  if (i.secretFindings > 0)\n    recs.push(`Rotate ${i.secretFindings} exposed secret(s) and purge from history.`);\n  if (i.auditFailures > 5) recs.push('Audit failures elevated — review auth/permission policies.');\n  if (score >= 85) recs.push('Posture healthy; maintain current controls.');\n  return recs;\n}\n\n/* Live signal gathering with graceful fallback (so unit tests with mocked\n * subsystems still get a deterministic snapshot). */\n\nasync function safe<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>, fallback: T): Promise<T> {\n  try {\n    return await fn();\n  } catch {\n    return fallback;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Contract entry point: compute the current posture snapshot from live\n * subsystems. Falls back to neutral signals if a subsystem is unavailable.\n */\nexport async function computePosture(): Promise<PostureReport> {\n  const dyn = async (spec: string): Promise<any> => {\n    try {\n      return await import(/* @vite-ignore */ spec);\n    } catch {\n      return {};\n    }\n  };\n  const [auditFailures, activeAnomalies, incidents, siem, secretFindings, breachEvents] =\n    await Promise.all([\n      safe(async () => (await dyn('./audit-analytics.js')).countEvents?.('auth_failure') ?? 0, 0),\n      safe(async () => (await dyn('./anomaly-detector.js')).getActiveAnomalies?.()?.length ?? 0, 0),\n      safe(\n        async () => {\n          const list = (await dyn('./incident-response.js')).listIncidents?.() ?? Anomaly detection (conflicting memories, data drift)\n * - Trend tracking (activity patterns over time)\n * - Implicit conclusion generation (derive new facts from existing data)\n * - Gap analysis (identify missing skills or memories)\n * - Shadow canary analysis (REAL, data-derived strategy promotion)\n *\n * Runs as a daemon agent at ring 4 (lowest priority / no tool access).\n */\n\nimport { db } from '../db/client.js';\nimport { log } from '../lib/logging.js';\nimport { and, eq, gte } from 'drizzle-orm';\nimport { memories, agentTasks, auditLog } from '../db/client.js';\n\n/* ── Shadow Analysis Results ── */\n\nexport interface ShadowInsight {\n  type: 'anomaly' | 'trend' | 'implicit_conclusion' | 'gap';\n  severity: 'info' | 'warning' | 'critical';\n  title: string;\n  detail: string;\n  relatedIds?: string[];\n}\n\nexport interface ShadowReport {\n  insights: ShadowInsight[];\n  runDurationMs: number;\n}\n\n/* ── Main Daemon Entrypoint ── */\n\n/**\n * Run a full shadow cognition cycle.\n * Designed to be called from the worker maintenance loop.\n */\nexport async function runShadowCycle(): Promise<ShadowReport> {\n  const start = Date.now();\n  const insights: ShadowInsight[] = [];\n\n  try {\n    const [anomalies, trends, conclusions, gaps] = await Promise.all([\n      detectAnomalies(),\n      trackTrends(),\n      generateImplicitConclusions(),\n      analyzeGaps(),\n    ]);\n\n    insights.push(...anomalies, ...trends, ...conclusions, ...gaps);\n\n    if (insights.length > 0) {\n      log.info('shadow_cycle_complete', {\n        insightCount: insights.length,\n        durationMs: Date.now() - start,\n      });\n    }\n  } catch (e) {\n    log.error('shadow_cycle_failed', { error: e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e) });\n  }\n\n  return { insights, runDurationMs: Date.now() - start };\n}\n\n/* ── Anomaly Detection ── */\n\nasync function detectAnomalies(): Promise<ShadowInsight[]> {\n  const insights: ShadowInsight[] = [];\n  const SEVEN_DAYS_AGO = new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 3600_000).toISOString();\n\n  // 1. Detect conflicting memories: same entity, opposite assertions\n  const recentMemories = await db\n    .select()\n    .from(memories)\n    .where(gte(memories.createdAt, SEVEN_DAYS_AGO))\n    .limit(500);\n\n  const byContent: Map<string, typeof recentMemories> = new Map();\n  for (const m of recentMemories) {\n    const key = m.title.toLowerCase().slice(0, 40);\n    if (!byContent.has(key)) byContent.set(key, []);\n    byContent.get(key)!.push(m);\n  }\n\n  for (const [, group] of byContent) {\n    if (group.length < 2) continue;\n    const kinds = new Set(group.map((m: any) => m.kind));\n    if (kinds.size > 2) {\n      insights.push({\n        type: 'anomaly',\n        severity: 'warning',\n        title: 'Contradictory memory cluster detected',\n        detail: `${group.length} memories about \"${group[0]!.title}\" span ${kinds.size} different kinds (${[...kinds].join(', ')}). Possible fragment overlap.`,\n        relatedIds: group.map((m: any) => m.id),\n      });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // 2. Check for memory decay — many very low importance memories\n  const lowImportance = recentMemories.filter((m: any) => (m.importance ?? 0.5) < 0.15);\n  if (lowImportance.length > 20) {\n    insights.push({\n      type: 'anomaly',\n      severity: 'info',\n      title: 'Low-importance memory accumulation',\n      detail: `${lowImportance.length} memories in the last 7 days have importance < 0.15. Consider running compression.`,\n    });\n  }\n\n  return insights;\n}\n\n/* ── Trend Tracking ── */\n\nasync function trackTrends(): Promise<ShadowInsight[]> {\n  const insights: ShadowInsight[] = [];\n\n  try {\n    const SEVEN_DAYS_AGO = new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 3600_000).toISOString();\n    const THIRTY_DAYS_AGO = new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 * 3600_000).toISOString();\n\n    const [tasks7d, tasks30d, , topActionResult, successRateResult] = await Promise.all([\n      // Tasks in last 7 days\n      db\n        .select({ id: agentTasks.id })\n        .from(agentTasks)\n        .where(gte(agentTasks.createdAt, SEVEN_DAYS_AGO))\n        .then((r: any) => r.length),\n      // Tasks in last 30 days\n      db\n        .select({ id: agentTasks.id })\n        .from(agentTasks)\n        .where(gte(agentTasks.createdAt, THIRTY_DAYS_AGO))\n        .then((r: any) => r.length),\n      // Audit entries in last 7 days\n      db\n        .select({ id: auditLog.id, actor: auditLog.actor })\n        .from(auditLog)\n        .where(gte(auditLog.createdAt, SEVEN_DAYS_AGO))\n        .limit(100)\n        .then((r: any) => ({\n          count: r.length,\n          uniqueActors: new Set(r.map((x: { actor: string }) => x.actor)).size,\n        })),\n      // Most frequent action in last 7 days\n      (async () => {\n        const rows = await db\n          .select({ action: auditLog.action })\n          .from(auditLog)\n          .where(gte(auditLog.createdAt, SEVEN_DAYS_AGO))\n          .limit(100);\n        const counts = new Map<string, number>();\n        for (const r of rows) {\n          counts.set(r.action, (counts.get(r.action) ?? 0) + 1);\n        }\n        let top: string | null = null;\n        let topCount = 0;\n        for (const [action, count] of counts) {\n          if (count > topCount) {\n            top = action;\n            topCount = count;\n          }\n        }\n        return top;\n      })(),\n      // Task success rate\n      (async () => {\n        const success = await db\n          .select({ id: agentTasks.id })\n          .from(agentTasks)\n          .where(and(gte(agentTasks.createdAt, SEVEN_DAYS_AGO), eq(agentTasks.status, 'succeeded')))\n          .then((r: any) => r.length);\n        const failed = await db\n          .select({ id: agentTasks.id })\n          .from(agentTasks)\n          .where(and(gte(agentTasks.createdAt, SEVEN_DAYS_AGO), eq(agentTasks.status, 'failed')))\n          .then((r: any) => r.length);\n        const total = success + failed;\n        return total > 0 ? success / total : 1;\n      })(),\n    ]);\n\n    if (tasks7d === 0 && tasks30d === 0) {\n      insights.push({\n        type: 'trend',\n        severity: 'info',\n        title: 'System idle — no recent activity',\n        detail: 'No tasks were recorded in the last 30 days. The system may be in a dormant state.',\n      });\n    }\n\n    if (topActionResult) {\n      insights.push({\n        type: 'trend',\n        severity: 'info',\n        title: `Most frequent action: ${topActionResult}`,\n        detail: `${topActionResult} was the most common action in the last 7 days (${tasks7d} total tasks, ${(successRateResult * 100).toFixed(0)}% success rate).`,\n      });\n    }\n  } catch {\n    // Non-critical — trends are best-effort\n  }\n\n  return insights;\n}\n\n/* ── Implicit Conclusions ── */\n\nasync function generateImplicitConclusions(): Promise<ShadowInsight[]> {\n  const insights: ShadowInsight[] = [];\n\n  try {\n    // Check for frequently paired tags across memories\n    const recentMemories = await db\n      .select()\n      .from(memories)\n      .where(gte(memories.createdAt, new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 * 3600_000).toISOString()))\n      .limit(200);\n\n    const tagPairs = new Map<string, number>();\n    for (const m of recentMemories) {\n      const tags = ((m.tags as string[]) ?? []).sort();\n      for (let i = 0; i < tags.length; i++) {\n        for (let j = i + 1; j < tags.length; j++) {\n          const key = `${tags[i]}::${tags[j]}`;\n          tagPairs.set(key, (tagPairs.get(key) ?? 0) + 1);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    let maxPairs = 0;\n    let maxPairKey = '';\n    for (const [key, count] of tagPairs) {\n      if (count > maxPairs) {\n        maxPairs = count;\n        maxPairKey = key;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (maxPairs >= 3 && maxPairKey) {\n      const [tagA, tagB] = maxPairKey.split('::');\n      insights.push({\n        type: 'implicit_conclusion',\n        severity: 'info',\n        title: `Strong tag correlation: #${tagA} ↔ #${tagB}`,\n        detail: `These tags co-occur in ${maxPairs} memories — suggesting an implicit relationship to record as a semantic link.`,\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Memory kind distribution\n    const kindCounts = new Map<string, number>();\n    for (const m of recentMemories) {\n      kindCounts.set(m.kind, (kindCounts.get(m.kind) ?? 0) + 1);\n    }\n    const dominantKind = [...kindCounts.entries()].sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0];\n    if (dominantKind && dominantKind[1] > recentMemories.length * 0.6) {\n      insights.push({\n        type: 'implicit_conclusion',\n        severity: 'info',\n        title: `Memory kind skew: ${dominantKind[0]} dominates`,\n        detail: `${dominantKind[0]} memories make up ${((dominantKind[1] / recentMemories.length) * 100).toFixed(0)}% of recent entries. Other kinds may be underrepresented.`,\n      });\n    }\n  } catch {\n    // Non-critical\n  }\n\n  return insights;\n}\n\n/* ── Gap Analysis ── */\n\nasync function analyzeGaps(): Promise<ShadowInsight[]> {\n  const insights: ShadowInsight[] = [];\n\n  try {\n    const recentSkills = await db\n      .select()\n      .from(memories)\n      .where(\n        and(\n          eq(memories.kind, 'skill'),\n          gte(memories.createdAt, new Date(Date.now() - 14 * 24 * 3600_000).toISOString())\n        )\n      )\n      .limit(100);\n\n    if (recentSkills.length === 0) {\n      insights.push({\n        type: 'gap',\n        severity: 'warning',\n        title: 'No skills recorded recently',\n        detail:\n          'No skill-type memories have been recorded in the last 14 days. (JSON.stringify(extractShape(inputs[i])) !== firstInputShape) {\r\n      return false;\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  return true;\r\n}\r\n\r\n// ── Script Generation ─────────────────────────────────────────\r\n\r\nexport interface GeneratedScript {\r\n  signature: string;\r\n  taskLabel: string;\r\n  code: string;\r\n  language: string;\r\n  estimatedTokensSaved: number;\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * Generate a deterministic JavaScript function from the detected pattern.\r\n *\r\n * This uses a template-based approach (not LLM) to produce a safe,\r\n * predictable * backslashes so untrusted pattern fields can never break out of the comment\r\n * and inject executable code into a generated skill (template-injection guard).\r\n */\r\nfunction sanitizeForComment(s: unknown): string {\r\n  return String(s)\r\n    .replace(/\\*\\//g, '* /')\r\n    .replace(/\\/\\*/g, '/ *')\r\n    .replace(/[\\r\\n]/g, ' ');\r\n}\r\n  const inputKeys = function based on the observed mapping\r\n  const code = `/**\r\n * Auto-compiled by NEXUS Neural Skill Compiler\r\n * Pattern: \r\n * Detected: ${pattern.occurrences} repetitions\r\n * Avg tokens/call: ${pattern.avgTokensPerCall}\r\n * Avg latency: ${pattern.avgLatencyMs}ms\r\n *\r\n * This function replaces the LLM reasoning chain for this task pattern.\r\n * It is a deterministic mapping from input to output, validated against\r\n * ${pattern.sampleInputs.length} historical examples.\r\n *\r\n * Compiled at: ${new Date().toISOString()}\r\n */\r\nfunction compiledTask(input) {\r\n  // Extract input fields\r\n  ${inputKeys.map((k: any) => `const ${k.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_')} = input[\"${k}\"];`).join('\\n  ')}\r\n\r\n  // Deterministic transformation (extracted from pattern analysis)\r\n  // NOTE: This is a structural mapping. If the task involves complex\r\n  // reasoning that varies per input, this compiled function should be\r\n  // deprecated and the LLM call restored.\r\n  const output = {\r\n    ${outputKeys.map((k: testResults = ;\r\n\r\nmodule.exports = { compiledTask, testResults };\r\n`;\r\n\r\n  return {\r\n    signature: pattern.signature,\r\n    taskLabel: pattern.taskLabel,\r\n    code,\r\n    language: 'javascript',\r\n    estimatedTokensSaved: pattern.avgTokensPerCall * pattern.occurrences,\r\n  };\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * Infer the simplest expression that produces the output field.\r\n * For truly deterministic tasks, the output is often a direct mapping\r\n * or simple transformation of an input field.\r\n */\r\nfunction inferOutputExpression(\r\n  outputKey: string,\r\n  inputKeys: string[],\r\n  pattern: DetectedPattern\r\n): string {\r\n  // Check if output key matches an input key (direct mapping)\r\n  if (inputKeys.includes(outputKey)) {\r\n    return outputKey.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_');\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  // Check if the output values are constant across all samples\r\n  const outputValues = pattern.sampleOutputs\r\n    .map((o: any) => (o as Record<string, unknown>)?.[outputKey])\r\n    .filter((v: any) => v !== undefined);\r\n\r\n  if (outputValues.length >= 2) {\r\n    const allSame = outputValues.every(\r\n      (v: any) => marked as \"needs LLM\")\r\n  return 'null /* requires-llm: output is not deterministic */';\r\n}\r\n\r\n// ── Evaluation ────────────────────────────────────────────────\r\n\r\nexport interface against historical sample data.\r\n * Runs the compiled function on each sample input and compares\r\n * the output against the historical output.\r\n *\r\n * Returns pass=true only if 100% of samples match.\r\n */\r\nexport async function evaluateScript(\r\n  script: GeneratedScript,\r\n  pattern: DetectedPattern\r\n): Promise<EvalScriptResult> {\r\n  const details: string[] = [];\r\n  let correct = 0;\r\n  const total = Math.min(pattern.sampleInputs.length, pattern.sampleOutputs.length);\r\n\r\n  for (let i = 0; i < total; i++) {\r\n    const expected = pattern.sampleOutputs[i];\r\n    try {\r\n      // Evaluate via sandbox (Docker if available, in-process fallback)\r\n      const { executeSandboxed } = await import('./sandbox.js');\r\n      const sandboxResult = await JSON.stringify(sandboxResult.output) === JSON.stringify(expected);\r\n      if (isMatch) {\r\n        correct++;\r\n        details.push(`✓ Sample ${i + 1}: MATCH`);\r\n      } else {\r\n        details.push(\r\n          `✕ Sample ${i + 1}: MISMATCH (expected ${JSON.stringify(expected).slice(0, 80)}, got ${JSON.stringify(sandboxResult.output).slice(0, 80)})`\r\n        );\r\n      }\r\n    } catch (e) {\r\n      details.push(`✕ Sample ${i + 1}: ERROR (${e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e)})`);\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  const matchRate = total > 0 ? correct / total : 0;\r\n  return {\r\n    passed: matchRate >= EVAL_MATCH_THRESHOLD,\r\n    matchRate,\r\n    testedSamples: total,\r\n    correctOutputs: correct,\r\n    details,\r\n  };\r\n}\r\n\r\n// ── Compilation Pipeline ──────────────────────────────────────\r\n\r\nexport interface CompilationResult {\r\n  detected: number;\r\n  compiled: number;\r\n  activated: number;\r\n  skipped: number;\r\n  results: Array<{\r\n number;\r\n  }>;\r\n}\r\n// ── Sandbox dry-run: capability validation (fail-closed) ─────────────────\r\n\r\n/** Thrown when a compiled skill attempts a capability it is not granted. */\r\nexport class SkillCapabilityViolation extends Error {\r\n  constructor(\r\n    public readonly capability: string,\r\n    public readonly declared: string[]\r\n  ) {\r\n    super(\r\n      `skill capability 'recall.write',\r\n];\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * Fail-closed validation: every capability a skill attempts must be granted\r\n * by its declared spec. `declared` is the allow-list the skill published;\r\n * validateSkillCapabilities(declared: string[], attempted: string[]): void {\r\n  const specs: CapabilitySpec[] = declared.map((d) =>\r\n    d.endsWith('.') ? { prefix: d } : { exact: d }\r\n  );\r\n  const fakePlugin = { manifest: { capabilities: specs } } as unknown as LoadedPlugin;\r\n  for (const cap of attempted) {\r\n    if (checkCapability(fakePlugin, cap) == null) {\r\n      throw new This is the sandbox dry-run gate run BEFORE publish/\r\n * activation so a skill that reaches for undeclared powers fails closed.\r\n */\r\nexport function dryRunSkill(code: string, sampleInputs: unknown[]): string[] {\r\n  const attempted = new Set<string>();\r\n  const sandbox: Record<string, unknown> = {\r\n    requestCapability: (cap: string) => {\r\n      attempted.add(cap);\r\n      return true;\r\n    },\r\n    console: { log: () => undefined, error: () => undefined, warn: () => undefined },\r\n    Math,\r\n    JSON,\r\n    Date,\r\n    String,\r\n    Number,\r\n    Array,\r\n    Object,\r\n  };\r\n  for (const input of sampleInputs.slice(0, 3)) {\r\n    const ctx = { ...sandbox, input } as unknown as Context;\r\n    try {\r\n      runInNewContext(`(function(){ ${code} })()`, ctx, { timeout: 2000 });\r\n    } catch {\r\n      /* Execution errors are surfaced by the eval harness; we only track caps. */\r\n    }\r\n  }\r\n  return [...attempted];\r\n}\r\n\r\n/**\r\n * Run the full Neural Skill Compilation pipeline:\r\n *  1. avgLatencyMs: pattern.avgLatencyMs,\r\n        activatedAt: evalResult.passed ? new Date() : null,\r\n      })\r\n      .onConflictDoNothing({ target: compiledScripts.patternSignature });\r\n\r\n      scriptId,\r\n          pattern: pattern.signature,\r\n          label: pattern.taskLabel,\r\n          occurrences: pattern.occurrences,\r\n          tokensSaved: script.estimatedTokensSaved,\r\n tokens.\r\n *\r\n * Returns the compiled output, or null if no script matches.\r\n */\r\nexport async function checkCompiledScript(\r\n  taskLabel: string,\r\n  input: unknown\r\n): Promise<{ output: const result = await executeSandboxed({\r\n      code: script.script,\r\n      language: script.language,\r\n      input,\r\n      timeoutMs: 30_000,\r\n    });\r\n\r\n    if (!result.ok) {\r\n script.id));\r\n      return null;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    await db\r\n      .update(compiledScripts)\r\n      .set({\r\n        timesExecuted: script.timesExecuted + 1,\r\n        updatedAt: new Date(),\r\n      })\r\n      .where(eq(compiledScripts.id, script.id));\r\n\r\n    return { output: result.output, scriptId: script.id };\r\n  } catch {\r\n    await db\r\n      .update(compiledScripts)\r\n      .set({\r\n        status: 'deprecated',\r\n        updatedAt: new Date(),\r\n      })\r\n      .where(eq(compiledScripts.id, script.id));\r\n    return null;\r\n  }\r\n}\r\n\r\n/** List all compiled scripts (for the dashboard). */\r\nexport async function listCompiledScripts() {\r\n  return Extracts the common input/output shape\n *   2. Generates a deterministic JS function to perform that transformation\n *   3. Runs it through the eval harness (compares against historical outputs)\n *   4. If 100% match → activates the script and hot-swaps the LLM call\n *\n * This permanently replaces expensive LLM reasoning with native code for\n * deterministic tasks, drastically reducing token spend and latency.\n */\nimport { db } from '../db/client.js';\nimport { trajectoryLogs, agentTasks, compiledScripts } from '../db/client.js';\nimport { appendAudit } from '../lib/audit.js';\nimport { eq, desc, and, gte } from 'drizzle-orm';\nimport { randomUUID, createHash } from 'node:crypto';\nimport { env } from '../lib/env.js';\n\n// Environment overrides are strings; parse defensively so thresholds are real\n// numbers (a raw string would make `count >= threshold` compare string-vs-number,\n// and `if (threshold)` would always be truthy). Defaults: 5 repetitions to compile,\n// 100% (1.0) exact-match ratio required to activate a compiled script.\nconst COMPILATION_THRESHOLD = Number(env.NEXUS_COMPILATION_THRESHOLD) || 5;\nconst EVAL_MATCH_THRESHOLD = (() => {\n  const raw = Number(env.NEXUS_EVAL_MATCH_THRESHOLD);\n  return Number.isFinite(raw) && raw > 0 ? raw : 1.0;\n})();\n\n// ── Pattern Detection ─────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport interface DetectedPattern {\n  signature: string;\n  taskLabel: string;\n  inputShape: unknown;\n  outputShape: unknown;\n  occurrences: number;\n  avgTokensPerCall: number;\n  avgLatencyMs: number;\n  sampleInputs: unknown[];\n  sampleOutputs: unknown[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Scan recent audit logs for repetitive task patterns.\n * Groups by task label + input shape similarity.\n * Returns patterns that exceed the compilation threshold.\n */\nexport async function detectRepetitivePatterns(): Promise<DetectedPattern[]> {\n  // Get recent successful tasks with their trajectories (last 7 days)\n  const recentTasks = await db\n    .select({\n      id: agentTasks.id,\n      label: agentTasks.label,\n      input: agentTasks.input,\n      output: agentTasks.output,\n      status: agentTasks.status,\n      createdAt: agentTasks.createdAt,\n    })\n    .from(agentTasks)\n    .where(\n      and(\n        eq(agentTasks.status, 'succeeded'),\n        gte(agentTasks.createdAt, new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86_400_000))\n      )\n    )\n    .orderBy(desc(agentTasks.createdAt))\n    .limit(500);\n\n  // Group by normalized label (strip IDs, timestamps, etc.)\n  const groups = new Map<string, typeof recentTasks>();\n  for (const task of recentTasks) {\n    const normalized = normalizeLabel(task.label);\n    const existing = groups.get(normalized) ?? [];\n    existing.push(task);\n    groups.set(normalized, existing);\n  }\n\n  // Find groups with >= threshold repetitions\n  const patterns: DetectedPattern[] = [];\n  for (const [normalizedLabel, tasks] of groups) {\n    if (tasks.length < COMPILATION_THRESHOLD) continue;\n\n    // Extract input/output shapes from samples\n    const sampleInputs = tasks.slice(0, 10).map((t: any) => t.input);\n    const sampleOutputs = tasks.slice(0, 10).map((t: any) => t.output);\n\n    // Check if outputs are structurally similar (deterministic transformation)\n    const inputShape = extractShape(sampleInputs[0]);\n    const outputShape = extractShape(sampleOutputs[0]);\n\n    // Only compile if input→output is a deterministic mapping\n    if (!isDeterministicTransformation(sampleInputs, sampleOutputs)) continue;\n\n    // Get token usage from trajectories\n    const tokenUsages = await db\n      .select({ tokenUsage: trajectoryLogs.tokenUsage, latencyMs: trajectoryLogs.latencyMs })\n      .from(trajectoryLogs)\n      .innerJoin(agentTasks, eq(trajectoryLogs.auditSequence, agentTasks.id))\n      .where(and(eq(agentTasks.label, tasks[0]!.label), eq(agentTasks.status, 'succeeded')))\n      .limit(tasks.length);\n\n    const totalTokens = tokenUsages.reduce((sum: number, t: any) => {\n      const usage = t.tokenUsage as { total?: number } | null;\n      return sum + (usage?.total ?? 0);\n    }, 0);\n    const totalLatency = tokenUsages.reduce((sum: number, t: any) => sum + t.latencyMs, 0);\n\n    patterns.push({\n      signature: createHash('sha256').update(normalizedLabel).digest('hex').slice(0, 16),\n      taskLabel: normalizedLabel,\n      inputShape,\n      outputShape,\n      occurrences: tasks.length,\n      avgTokensPerCall: tokenUsages.length > 0 ? Math.round(totalTokens / tokenUsages.length) : 0,\n      avgLatencyMs: tokenUsages.length > 0 ? Math.round(totalLatency / tokenUsages.length) : 0,\n      sampleInputs,\n      sampleOutputs,\n    });\n  }\n\n  return patterns.sort((a, b) => b.occurrences - a.occurrences);\n}\n\n/** Normalize a task label by stripping dynamic content (IDs, timestamps). */\nfunction normalizeLabel(label: string): string {\n  return label\n    .replace(/[a-f0-9]{8}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{12}/gi, '{uuid}') // UUIDs\n    .replace(/\\\\d{10,}/g, '{timestamp}') // Unix timestamps\n    .replace(/\\\\b\\\\d+\\\\b/g, '{n}') // Generic numbers\n    .replace(/\\\\b[A-Z]{2,}_\\\\w+/g, '{env_var}') // ENV_VAR patterns\n    .trim()\n    .toLowerCase();\n}\n\n/** Extract the structural shape of a value (keys + types, not values). */\nfunction extractShape(value: unknown): unknown {\n  if (value === null || value === undefined) return 'null';\n  if (typeof value !== 'object') return typeof value;\n  if (Array.isArray(value)) {\n    return value.length > 0 ? [extractShape(value[0])] : [];\n  }\n  const result: Record<string, unknown> = {};\n  for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(value as Record<string, unknown>)) {\n    result[k] = extractShape(v);\n  }\n  return result;\n}\n\n/**\n * Check if the input→output mapping is deterministic.\n * If the same input always produces the same output structure, it's\n * a good candidate for compilation (the transformation is predictable).\n */\nfunction isDeterministicTransformation(inputs: unknown[], outputs: unknown[]): boolean {\n  if (inputs.length < 2 || outputs.length < 2) return false;\n\n  // Check that all outputs have the same structural shape\n  const firstOutputShape = JSON.stringify(extractShape(outputs[0]));\n  for (let i = 1; i < outputs.length; i++) {\n    if (JSON.stringify(extractShape(outputs[i])) !== firstOutputShape) {\n      return false; // outputs have different shapes — not deterministic\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Check that all inputs have the same structural shape\n  const firstInputShape = JSON.stringify(extractShape(inputs[0]));\n  for (let i = 1; i < inputs.length; i++) {\n    if (JSON.stringify(extractShape(inputs[i])) !== firstInputShape) {\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return true;\n}\n\n// ── Script Generation ─────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport interface GeneratedScript {\n  signature: string;\n  taskLabel: string;\n  code: string;\n  language: string;\n  estimatedTokensSaved: number;\n}\n\n/**\n * Generate a deterministic JavaScript function from the detected pattern.\n *\n * This uses a template-based approach (not LLM) to produce a safe,\n * predictable function that maps the input shape to the output shape.\n * The generated code is stored and validated before activation.\n */\nexport function generateScript(pattern: DetectedPattern): GeneratedScript {\n  const inputKeys = Object.keys((pattern.inputShape as Record<string, unknown>) ?? {});\n  const outputKeys = Object.keys((pattern.outputShape as Record<string, unknown>) ?? {});\n\n  // Generate a transformation function based on the observed mapping\n  const code = `/**\n * Auto-compiled by NEXUS Neural Skill Compiler\n * Pattern: ${pattern.taskLabel}\n * Detected: ${pattern.occurrences} repetitions\n * Avg tokens/call: ${pattern.avgTokensPerCall}\n * Avg latency: ${pattern.avgLatencyMs}ms\n *\n * This function replaces the LLM reasoning chain for this task pattern.\n * It is a deterministic mapping from input to output, validated against\n * ${pattern.sampleInputs.length} historical examples.\n *\n * Compiled at: ${new Date().toISOString()}\n */\nfunction compiledTask(input) {\n  // Extract input fields\n  ${inputKeys.map((k: any) => `const ${k.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_')} = input[\"${k}\"];`).join('\\n  ')}\n\n  // Deterministic transformation (extracted from pattern analysis)\n  // NOTE: This is a structural mapping. If the task involves complex\n  // reasoning that varies per input, this compiled function should be\n  // deprecated and the LLM call restored.\n  const output = {\n    ${outputKeys.map((k: any) => `\"${k}\": ${inferOutputExpression(k, inputKeys, pattern)}`).join(',\\n    ')}\n  };\n\n  return output;\n}\n\n// Self-test: verify against historical samples\nconst testResults = ${JSON.stringify(pattern.sampleOutputs.slice(0, 3), null, 2)};\n\nmodule.exports = { compiledTask, testResults };\n`;\n\n  return {\n    signature: pattern.signature,\n    taskLabel: pattern.taskLabel,\n    code,\n    language: 'javascript',\n    estimatedTokensSaved: pattern.avgTokensPerCall * pattern.occurrences,\n  };\n}\n\n/**\n * Infer the simplest expression that produces the output field.\n * For truly deterministic tasks, the output is often a direct mapping\n * or simple transformation of an input field.\n */\nfunction inferOutputExpression(\n  outputKey: string,\n  inputKeys: string[],\n  pattern: DetectedPattern\n): string {\n  // Check if output key matches an input key (direct mapping)\n  if (inputKeys.includes(outputKey)) {\n    return outputKey.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_');\n  }\n\n  // Check if the output values are constant across all samples\n  const outputValues = pattern.sampleOutputs\n    .map((o: any) => (o as Record<string, unknown>)?.[outputKey])\n    .filter((v: any) => v !== undefined);\n\n  if (outputValues.length >= 2) {\n    const allSame = outputValues.every(\n      (v: any) => JSON.stringify(v) === JSON.stringify(outputValues[0])\n    );\n    if (allSame) {\n      return JSON.stringify(outputValues[0]);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Default: null (will fail eval and be marked as \"needs LLM\")\n  return 'null /* requires-llm: output is not deterministic */';\n}\n\n// ── Evaluation ────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport interface EvalScriptResult {\n  passed: boolean;\n  matchRate: number;\n  testedSamples: number;\n  correctOutputs: number;\n  details: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Evaluate a generated script against historical sample data.\n * Runs the compiled function on each sample input and compares\n * the output against the historical output.\n *\n * Returns pass=true only if 100% of samples match.\n */\nexport async function evaluateScript(\n  script: GeneratedScript,\n  pattern: DetectedPattern\n): Promise<EvalScriptResult> {\n  const details: string[] = [];\n  let correct = 0;\n  const total = Math.min(pattern.sampleInputs.length, pattern.sampleOutputs.length);\n\n  for (let i = 0; i < total; i++) {\n    const expected = pattern.sampleOutputs[i];\n    try {\n      // Evaluate via sandbox (Docker if available, in-process fallback)\n      const { executeSandboxed } = await import('./sandbox.js');\n      const sandboxResult = await executeSandboxed({\n        code: script.code,\n        language: 'javascript',\n        input: pattern.sampleInputs[i],\n      });\n\n      const isMatch = JSON.stringify(sandboxResult.output) === JSON.stringify(expected);\n      if (isMatch) {\n        correct++;\n        details.push(`✓ Sample ${i + 1}: MATCH`);\n      } else {\n        details.push(\n          `✕ Sample ${i + 1}: MISMATCH (expected ${JSON.stringify(expected).slice(0, 80)}, got ${JSON.stringify(sandboxResult.output).slice(0, 80)})`\n        );\n      }\n    } catch (e) {\n      details.push(`✕ Sample ${i + 1}: ERROR (${e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e)})`);\n    }\n  }\n\n  const matchRate = total > 0 ? correct / total : 0;\n  return {\n    passed: matchRate >= EVAL_MATCH_THRESHOLD,\n    matchRate,\n    testedSamples: total,\n    correctOutputs: correct,\n    details,\n  };\n}\n\n// ── Compilation Pipeline ────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport interface CompilationResult {\n  detected: number;\n  compiled: number;\n  activated: number;\n  skipped: number;\n  results: Array<{\n    pattern: string;\n    label: string;\n    occurrences: number;\n    status: 'compiled' | 'skipped_inconsistent' | 'skipped_existing' | 'eval_failed' | 'activated';\n    tokensSaved?: number;\n  }>;\n}\n\n/**\n * Run the full Neural Skill Compilation pipeline:\n *   1. Connection reuse — a shared semaphore bounds the number of concurrent\n *     outbound connections to LLM providers. Because the Node global `fetch`\n *     already keeps an internal keep-alive pool, funnelling every call through a\n *     single acquire/release path maximizes connection reuse (hot connections\n *     stay open instead of being opened per-call) and prevents connection\n *     exhaustion under burst. When `undici` is importable it is used to attach\n *     an explicit keep-alive `Agent` dispatcher; otherwise the module degrades\n *     gracefully to the default global pool.\n *\n *  2. This applies upstream\n *     pressure and prevents the runtime from overwhelming providers (or the\n *     local file descriptor limit). The same primitive is reused by the agent\n *     runtime dispatch loop for bounded fan-out.\n */\n\ntype Dispatcher = unknown;\n\nfunction debugLog(_msg: string, _ctx?: Record<string, unknown>): void {\n  if (process.env.NEXUS_DEBUG) {\n    // eslint-disable-next-line no-console\n    console.debug(`[conn-pool] ${_msg}`, _ctx ?? Matches the convention used by\n  // the audit chain's `stableStringify`.\n  return JSON.stringify(m, Object.keys(m).sort());\n}\n\nexport function verifyManifestSignature(\n  manifest: PluginManifest,\n  signatureB64: string,\n  publisherPubkeyB64: string\n): boolean {\n  try {\n    const msg = Buffer.from(canonicalizeManifest(manifest), 'utf8');\n    const sig = Buffer.from(signatureB64, 'base64');\n    const pub = Buffer.from(publisherPubkeyB64, 'base64');\n    return verify(null, msg, { key: pub, format: 'der', type: 'spki' }, sig);\n  } catch (e) {\n    log.warn('plugin.signature_verify_failed', {\n      error: e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e),\n    });\n    return false;\n  }\n}\n\n/* ─── Install / uninstall / load ─────────────────────────────────────────── */\n\nexport async function registerPlugin(input: {\n  name: string;\n  version: string;\n  description?: string;\n  authorPubkey: string;\n  signature: string;\n  wasmBytes: Uint8Array;\n  manifest: PluginManifest;\n  homepage?: string;\n  license?: string;\n  source?: string;\n}): Promise<LoadedPlugin> {\n  // 1. validate the manifest schema\n  const validated = validateManifest(input.manifest);\n\n  // 2. verify signature\n  if (!verifyManifestSignature(validated, input.signature, input.authorPubkey)) {\n    await appendAudit(\n      'plugin.signature_invalid',\n      { name: input.name, version: input.version },\n      'plugin-runtime'\n    );\n    throw new Error('plugin_signature_invalid');\n  }\n\n  // 3. compute content hash\n  const contentSha256 = createHash('sha256').update(input.wasmBytes).digest('hex');\n\n  // 4. trust assignment\n  const trustState: 'trusted' | 'untrusted' = TRUSTED_PUBLISHERS.has(input.authorPubkey)\n    ? 'trusted'\n    : 'untrusted';\n\n  // 5. upsert\n  const id = `plg_${randomUUID()}`;\n  await db\n    .insert(plugins)\n    .values({\n      id,\n      name: input.name,\n      version: input.version,\n      description: input.description ?? '',\n      authorPubkey: input.authorPubkey,\n      signature: input.signature,\n      contentSha256,\n      manifest: validated as unknown as Record<string, unknown>,\n      wasmBytes: Buffer.from(input.wasmBytes).toString('base64'),\n      source: input.source ?? 'local',\n      homepage: input.homepage ?? null,\n      license: input.license ?? null,\n      ratingAvg: 0,\n      ratingCount: 0,\n      installCount: 0,\n      trustState,\n      createdAt: new Date(),\n      updatedAt: new Date(),\n    })\n    .onConflictDoNothing();\n\n  await appendAudit(\n    'plugin.registered',\n    {\n      name: input.name,\n      version: input.version,\n      contentSha256,\n      trustState,\n      publisherTrusted: TRUSTED_PUBLISHERS.has(input.authorPubkey),\n    },\n    'plugin-runtime'\n  );\n\n  log.info('plugin.registered', { id, name: input.name, version: input.version, trustState });\n  const loaded = await loadPlugin(id);\n  if (!loaded) throw new Error('plugin_load_failed');\n  return loaded;\n}\n\nexport async function installPlugin(\n  pluginId: string,\n  opts?: { ringOverride?: number; config?: Record<string, unknown> }\n): Promise<void> {\n  const plugin = await loadPlugin(pluginId);\n  if (!plugin) throw new Error('plugin_not_found');\n  if (plugin.trustState === 'revoked') throw new Error('plugin_revoked');\n\n  const installId = `pi_${randomUUID()}`;\n  await db\n    .insert(pluginInstallations)\n    .values({\n      id: installId,\n      pluginId,\n      enabled: true,\n      ringOverride: opts?.ringOverride ?? null,\n      config: opts?.config ?? {},\n      installedAt: new Date(),\n      updatedAt: new Date(),\n    })\n    .onConflictDoUpdate({\n      target: pluginInstallations.pluginId,\n      set: {\n        enabled: true,\n        ringOverride: opts?.ringOverride ?? null,\n        config: opts?.config ?? {},\n        updatedAt: new Date(),\n      },\n    });\n\n  await db\n    .update(plugins)\n    .set({\n      installCount:\n        (await db.query.plugins.findFirst({ where: eq(plugins.id, pluginId) }))!.installCount + 1,\n      updatedAt: new Date(),\n    })\n    .where(eq(plugins.id, pluginId));\n  await appendAudit(\n    'plugin.installed',\n    { pluginId, installId, ringOverride: opts?.ringOverride ?? null },\n    'plugin-runtime'\n  );\n  loaded.delete(pluginId); // force re-load with new config\n}\n\nexport async function uninstallPlugin(pluginId: string): Promise<void> {\n  await db\n    .update(pluginInstallations)\n    .set({ enabled: false, updatedAt: new Date() })\n    .where(eq(pluginInstallations.pluginId, pluginId));\n  await appendAudit('plugin.uninstalled', { pluginId }, 'plugin-runtime');\n  loaded.delete(pluginId);\n}\n\n/* ─── Integrity gate + resource fuse (self-healing isolation) ─────────────── */\n\n/**\n * Artifact integrity / attestation check (fail-closed).\n *\n * 1. Checksum: recompute the SHA-256 of the plugin's recorded WASM bytes and\n *    compare against the stored `contentSha256`. A mismatch means the artifact\n *    was tampered with on disk or in the DB and MUST NOT be executed.\n * 2. Attestation: if a publisher Ed25519 public key is registered for the\n *    plugin's author (`publisherPubKeys` map), verify the manifest signature\n *    over the manifest body. Missing/unverifiable signatures on an attested\n *    publisher are rejected.\n *\n * Returns a report; throws `IntegrityGateFailure` when the artifact must not\n * be executed (default-deny — never silently proceed).\n */\nexport interface IntegrityReport {\n  checkedAt: number;\n  checksumOk: boolean;\n  attested: boolean;\n  attestedOk: boolean;\n  detail: string;\n}\n\nexport class IntegrityGateFailure extends Error {\n  constructor(public readonly report: IntegrityReport) {\n    super(`plugin integrity gate failed: ${report.detail}`);\n    this.name = 'IntegrityGateFailure';\n  }\n}\n\n/** Registered publisher -> Ed25519 public key (hex). Populated at boot/by operator. */\nexport const publisherPubKeys = new Map<string, string>();\n\nexport async function verifyArtifactIntegrity(plugin: LoadedPlugin): Promise<IntegrityReport> {\n  /** Read the persisted plugin row (artifact bytes + recorded hash) for integrity checks. */\n  async function getPluginRecord(\n    pluginId: string\n  ): Promise<{ contentSha256: string; wasmBytes?: Uint8Array } | null> {\n    const row = await db.query.plugins.findFirst({ where: eq(plugins.id, pluginId) });\n    if (!row) return null;\n    const bytes = row.wasmBytes ? Buffer.from(row.wasmBytes, 'base64') : undefined;\n    return { contentSha256: row.contentSha256, wasmBytes: bytes };\n  }\n\n  const recorded = await getPluginRecord(plugin.id);\n  const expectedSha = recorded?.contentSha256 ?? plugin.contentSha256;\n  const bytes = plugin.wasmBytes ?? recorded?.wasmBytes;\n  let checksumOk = false;\n  if (bytes && expectedSha) {\n    const actual = createHash('sha256').update(bytes).digest('hex');\n    checksumOk = actual === expectedSha;\n  }\n  const pubKey = plugin.manifest.author ? publisherPubKeys.get(plugin.manifest.author) : undefined;\n  let attested = false;\n  let attestedOk = false;\n  if (pubKey && plugin.manifest.signature) {\n    attested = true;\n    try {\n      const body = JSON.stringify({ ...plugin.manifest, signature: undefined });\n      const sig = Buffer.from(plugin.manifest.signature, 'hex');\n      const pkey = Buffer.from(pubKey, 'hex');\n      attestedOk = verify(null, Buffer.from(body, 'utf8'), pkey, sig);\n    } catch {\n      attestedOk = false;\n    }\n  }\n  const detail = !checksumOk\n    ? 'checksum mismatch or missing bytes/hash'\n    : attested && !attestedOk\n      ? 'publisher signature verification failed'\n      : 'ok';\n  const report: IntegrityReport = {\n    checkedAt: Date.now(),\n    checksumOk,\n    attested,\n    attestedOk: attested ? attestedOk : true,\n    detail,\n  };\n  if (!checksumOk || (attested && !attestedOk)) {\n    throw new IntegrityGateFailure(report);\n  }\n  return report;\n}\n\nexport interface ResourceFuseOptions {\n  timeoutMs: number;\n  maxFuel: number;\n}\n\nexport class ResourceFuseTripped extends Error {\n  constructor(\n    public readonly reason: 'timeout' | 'fuel',\n    public readonly limit: number\n  ) {\n    super(`resource fuse tripped: ${reason} (limit ${limit})`);\n    this.name = 'ResourceFuseTripped';\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Execute `fn` under a resource fuse. If the wall-clock `timeoutMs` elapses\n * before completion, the fuse trips (timeout) and we abort. Fuel is sampled\n * from `getFuel()` after the call returns; if it exceeds `maxFuel` the fuse\n * trips (fuel). This kills runaway WASM loops and feeds self-healing: callers\n * (invokePlugin) catch the trip and quarantine the plugin.\n */\nexport async function withResourceFuse<T>(\n  opts: ResourceFuseOptions,\n  fn: () => Promise<T>,\n  getFuel?: () => number\n): Promise<T> {\n  let timer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | undefined;\n  const timeoutPromise = new Promise<never>((_, reject) => {\n    timer = setTimeout(\n      () => reject(new ResourceFuseTripped('timeout', opts.timeoutMs)),\n      opts.timeoutMs\n    );\n  });\n  try {\n    const result = await Promise.race([fn(), timeoutPromise]);\n    if (getFuel) {\n      const fuel = getFuel();\n      if (fuel > opts.maxFuel) throw new ResourceFuseTripped('fuel', opts.maxFuel);\n    }\n    return result;\n  } finally {\n    if (timer) clearTimeout(timer);\n  }\n}\n\nexport async function loadPlugin(pluginId: string): Promise<LoadedPlugin | null> {\n  const cached = loaded.get(pluginId);\n  if (cached) return cached;\n\n  const row = await db.query.plugins.findFirst({ where: eq(plugins.id, pluginId) });\n  if (!row) return null;\n  const installRow = await db.query.pluginInstallations.findFirst({\n    where: eq(pluginInstallations.pluginId, pluginId),\n  });\n\n  const plugin: LoadedPlugin = {\n    id: row.id,\n    name: row.name,\n    version: row.version,\n    manifest: row.manifest as unknown as PluginManifest,\n    contentSha256: row.contentSha256,\n    wasmBytes: row.wasmBytes ? Buffer.from(row.wasmBytes, 'base64') : undefined,\n    trustState: row.trustState as 'untrusted' | 'trusted' | 'revoked',\n    ringOverride: installRow?.ringOverride ?? null,\n    config: (installRow?.config ?? {}) as Record<string, unknown>,\n  };\n  loaded.set(pluginId, plugin);\n  try {\n    await verifyArtifactIntegrity(plugin);\n  } catch (e) {\n    if (e instanceof IntegrityGateFailure) {\n      await db\n        .update(plugins)\n        .set({ trustState: 'revoked' })\n        .where(eq(plugins.id, plugin.id))\n        .catch(() => undefined);\n      throw new Error(`integrity_gate_failed:${plugin.id}:${e.report.detail}`);\n    }\n    throw e;\n  }\n  return plugin;\n}\n\n/**\n * Quarantine a plugin: revoke trust + disable its installation so it can no\n * longer be loaded or executed. Real self-healing on integrity/fuse breach.\n */\nexport async function quarantinePlugin(pluginId: string, reason: string): Promise<void> {\n  await db\n    .update(plugins)\n    .set({ trustState: 'revoked' })\n    .where(eq(plugins.id, pluginId))\n    .catch(() => undefined);\n  await db\n    .update(pluginInstallations)\n    .set({ disabled: true })\n    .where(eq(pluginInstallations.pluginId, pluginId))\n    .catch(() => undefined);\n  loaded.delete(pluginId);\n  appendAudit('plugin.quarantined', { pluginId, reason }, 'plugin-runtime').catch(() => undefined);\n}\n\nexport async function listInstalledPlugins(): Promise<LoadedPlugin[]> {\n  const installs = await db.query.pluginInstallations.findMany({\n    where: eq(pluginInstallations.enabled, true),\n  });\n  const out: LoadedPlugin[] = [];\n  for (const ins of installs) {\n    const p = await loadPlugin(ins.pluginId);\n    if (p) out.push(p);\n  }\n  return out;\n}\n\n/* ─── Capability check (default-deny) ────────────────────────────────────── */\n\nexport function checkCapability(plugin: LoadedPlugin, capability: string): CapabilitySpec | null {\n  let best: CapabilitySpec | null = null;\n  let bestScore = -1;\n  let bestDeny = false;\n  for (const spec of plugin.manifest.capabilities) {\n    const score = matchesCapability(spec, capability);\n    if (score == null) continue;\n    const isDeny = (spec.prefixExcept ?? []).some(\n      (exc) => capability === exc || capability.startsWith(exc + '.')\n    );\n    if (score > bestScore || (score === bestScore && isDeny && !bestDeny)) {\n      best = spec;\n      bestScore = score;\n      bestDeny = isDeny;\n    }\n  }\n  // A capability that only matches a deny (prefixExcept) rule grants nothing.\n  return bestDeny ? null : best;\n}\n\nfunction matchesCapability(spec: CapabilitySpec, requested: string): number | null {\n  if (spec.exact) {\n    return spec.exact === requested ? 1_000_000 + spec.exact.length : null;\n  }\n  if (!spec.prefix) return null;\n  const isExact = requested === spec.prefix;\n  const isChild = requested.startsWith(spec.prefix + '.');\n  if (!isExact && !isChild) return null;\n  const excepts = spec.prefixExcept ?? [];\n  const denied = excepts.some((exc) => requested === exc || requested.startsWith(exc + '.'));\n  return (denied ? 750_000 : 500_000) + spec.prefix.length;\n}\n/* ─── Invocation (the hot path) ──────────────────────────────────────────── */\n\nexport async function invokePlugin(req: PluginInvocation): Promise<PluginReceipt> {\n  const start = Date.now();\n  const inputSha256 = createHash('sha256').update(req.inputBytes).digest('hex');\n  const plugin = await loadPlugin(req.pluginId);\n  if (!plugin) throw new Error(`plugin_not_found:${req.pluginId}`);\n  if (plugin.trustState === 'revoked') throw new Error(`plugin_revoked:${req.pluginId}`);\n\n  const cap = checkCapability(plugin, req.capability);\n  if (!cap) {\n    const deniedId = `prc_${randomUUID()}`;\n    await db.insert(pluginReceipts).values({\n      id: deniedId,\n      pluginId: plugin.id,\n      installId: null,\n      agentId: req.agentId,\n      capability: req.capability,\n      inputSha256,\n      outputSha256: createHash('sha256').update(Buffer.from('denied', 'utf8')).digest('hex'),\n      exitCode: -13,\n      fuelUsed: 0,\n      durationMs: Date.now() - start,\n      authorized: false,\n      createdAt: new Date(),\n    });\n    await appendAudit(\n      'plugin.capability_denied',\n      {\n        pluginId: plugin.id,\n        agentId: req.agentId,\n        capability: req.capability,\n      },\n      'plugin-runtime'\n    );\n    throw new Error(`capability_denied:${req.capability}`);\n  }\n\n  const validated: ValidatedInvocation = { plugin, capability: cap, inputSha256, startedAt: start };\n  // Integrity gate before every execution (defense-in-depth; loadPlugin also checks).\n  await verifyArtifactIntegrity(plugin).catch((e) => {\n    if (e instanceof IntegrityGateFailure) {\n      throw new Error(`integrity_gate_failed:${plugin.id}:${e.report.detail}`);\n    }\n    throw e;\n  });\n\n  // Resource fuse: kill runaway WASM loops (wall-clock + fuel). null,\n    agentId: req.agentId,\n    capability: req.capability,\n    inputSha256,\n    outputSha256,\n    exitCode: result.exitCode,\n    fuelUsed: result.fuelUsed,\n    durationMs,\n    authorized: true,\n  };\n}\n\n/* ─── Receipts query (for the audit page) ───────────────────────────────── */\n\nexport async function listReceipts(opts?: {\n  pluginId?: string;\n  limit?: number;\n}): Promise<PluginReceipt[]> {\n  const rows = await db.query.pluginReceipts.findMany({\n    where: opts?.pluginId ? kernel.ts passes `new Date()`, `{…}`, `[…]` to text columns.\n  // This mapper converts to string; on read it returns the stored\n  // string as-is (no JSON.parse — avoids busting on CURRENT_TIMESTAMP defaults).\n  const safeText = (customType as any)({\n    dataType: () => 'text',\n    toDriver: (value: any) => {\n      if (value instanceof Date) return value.toISOString();\n      if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) return JSON.stringify(value);\n      if (value === undefined) return null;\n      return value;\n    },\n    fromDriver: (value: any) => value,\n  });\n\n  // ── Custom text-as-timestamp: stored as ISO string, read as Date ──\n  // kernel.ts code calls `.createdAt.getTime()` which requires a Date\n  // (PostgreSQL native behaviour), so we reconstruct Date on read.\n  const tsText = (customType as any)({\n    dataType: () => 'text',\n    toDriver: (value: Date) => {\n      if (value instanceof Date) return value.toISOString();\n      return String(value);\n    },\n    fromDriver: (value: string) => {\n      const d = new Date(String(value));\n      return Number.isNaN(d.getTime()) ? new Date(0) : d;\n    },\n  });\n\n  // ── Temp SQLite ────────────────────────────────────────\n  const tmpDir = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), 'nexus-kernel-test-'));\n  const dbPath = join(tmpDir, 'test.db');\n  const sqliteDb = new Database(dbPath);\n (existsSync(migrationPath)) {\n    for (const stmt of readFileSync(migrationPath, 'utf-8').split('--> statement-breakpoint')) {\n      const t = stmt.trim();\n      if (t) {\n        try {\n          sqliteDb.exec(t);\n        } catch (err: any) {\n          if (!String(err).includes('already exists')) throw err;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // ── Schema: agents .default(sql`(strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%fZ','now'))`),\n    updatedAt: tsText('updated_at')\n      .notNull()\n      .default(sql`(strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%fZ','now'))`),\n    lastHeartbeatAt: text('error'),\n    idempotencyKey: text('idempotency_key'),\n    retryCount: integer('retry_count').notNull().default(0),\n    maxRetries: integer('max_retries').notNull().default(3),\n    traceId: safeText('finished_at'),\n  });\n\n  const db = drizzle(sqliteDb, { schema: { agents, agentTasks } });\n  testRef.db = db;\n  testRef.agents = agents;\n  testRef.agentTasks = agentTasks;\n  testRef.sql = sql;\n\n  // Stub tables (not directly under test but needed for module completeness)\n  const apiKeys = sqliteTable('api_keys', {\n    id: text('id').primaryKey(),\n    name: 'shell')).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(1, 'memory.recall')).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(1, 'fs.read')).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(1, 'nexus_recall')).toBe(true);\n    });\n    it('ring 2 fallback grants all tools (PG dev target)', () => {\n      expect(checkACL(2, 'shell')).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(2, 'fs.write')).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(2, 'memory.recall')).toBe(true);\n    });\n    it('ring 3 is read-only (nexus_recall/nexus_stats only)', () => {\n      expect(checkACL(3, 'nexus_recall')).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(3, 'nexus_stats')).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(3, 'memory.recall')).toBe(false);\n      expect(checkACL(3, 'shell')).toBe(false);\n    });\n    it('ring 4 (quarantined) denies everything', () => {\n      expect(checkACL(4, 'nexus_recall')).toBe(false);\n      expect(checkACL(4, 'shell')).toBe(false);\n    });\n    it('minRing override: agentRing ≤ minRing → true', () => {\n      expect(checkACL(2, 'x', 2)).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(3, 'x', 3)).toBe(true);\n      expect(checkACL(3, 'x', 4)).toBe(true);\n    });\n    it('agentRing > minRing → false', () => {\n      expect(checkACL(3, 'x', 2)).toBe(false);\n      expect(checkACL(2, 'x', 1)).toBe(false);\n      expect(checkACL(4, 'x', 1)).toBe(false);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ──────────────────────
